[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/csv/TextAndCSVParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:200[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m204[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:                        cell = [0m[1;35mcellFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m201[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mxhtmlContentHandler.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m202[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mxhtmlContentHandler.characters[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m203[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mxhtmlContentHandler.endElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m204[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The timeout arises from the brute-force nested loops in CellFormatter.format [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which iterate over all denominator [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and numerator [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pairs up [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength−[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. For large denomLength [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this becomes effectively [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfinite, causing pathological CPU usage on crafted inputs.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The parsing loop in TextAndCSVParser.parse invokes CellFormatter.format on [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mevery cell, exacerbating the problem when the input contains many fraction-format [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcells.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Fix[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the brute-force search for the best rational approximation with an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mefficient continued-fraction-based algorithm that runs in [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlog N[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m time, where N is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe maximum denominator.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enforce a sane upper limit on denomLength [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to guard against [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munreasonably large patterns, with fallback to decimal formatting if the requested [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecision is too large.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserve existing functionality: inputs not matching the fraction pattern use [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same behavior; for fraction patterns, the output remains the closest possible [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfraction given the user’s template but computed efficiently.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Define MAX_DENOMINATOR_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconfigurable constant[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In CellFormatter.format:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After matching the fraction format, parse denomLength from the regex [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgroups.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - If denomLength > MAX_DENOMINATOR_LENGTH, log at debug level [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor silently[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand cap denomLength = MAX_DENOMINATOR_LENGTH.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Compute maxDenominator = [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength − [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Call a new private helper method `[0m[1;35mapproximateFraction[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble value, int [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxDenominator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` that implements the standard continued-fraction expansion [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • Iteratively build convergents until the next denominator would exceed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxDenominator.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • Compute the final best approximation by taking a linear combination of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe last two convergents.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • Return numerator and denominator as ints.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace the existing nested for-loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a single call to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis helper.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Keep the remaining formatting logic unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhole-part extraction, sign [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling, placeholder insertion[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to maintain existing output shape.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Add unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutside of harnesses[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to verify correctness for typical, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39medge, and oversize denomLength inputs. Since tests are not to be modified here, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure new code paths are covered by existing tests or add new ones in parser’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest suite if needed.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Non-fraction cells [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mfractionFormatMatcher.find[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m retain the exact [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame flow.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fraction patterns with small denomLength [0m[1;39m([0m[39m≤ [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m produce identical or [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnear-identical results to the original, since brute-force finds the mathematically [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moptimal approximation anyway.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Oversize denomLength requests degrade gracefully by capping precision rather [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan hanging.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness or fuzzing logic changes are required; existing fuzzer tests for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCSV parsing will still exercise the new algorithm but complete within time limits.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slight differences [0m[1;39m([0m[39min very rare cases[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m between continued-fraction and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrute-force results if multiple equally-close approximations exist. These [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdifferences are bounded by maxDenominator and are acceptable for CSV formatting.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Users requesting extremely high-precision fractions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenomLength > [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will see[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlower precision; document this cap in parser Javadocs.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Performance overhead of the continued-fraction algorithm is negligible [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompared to the original brute force.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References to Similar Code[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A comparable approach is used in Apache Commons Math’s Fraction class, but to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoid new dependencies, we implement a localized version following the standard [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Implementation Plan[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modify CellFormatter.java:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Add constants and helper method for continued fraction.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Replace lines [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[39m with a call to the helper.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Add input capping logic for denomLength.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing test suite to ensure no regressions.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that the fuzzer no longer times out on previously problematic inputs. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe project’s CSV parser fuzzer reported a libFuzzer timeout while exercising [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mCellFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. The fuzzer’s main thread was consuming excessive CPU [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtime inside `traceConstCmpInt` callbacks originating from `CellFormatter.format`. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo address performance concerns, a patch was attempted that replaces the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrute-force nested loops for computing the best fractional approximation with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinued-fraction algorithm [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`approximateFraction`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and limits the maximum [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdenominator length. Upon applying the patch, the build failed with dozens of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“illegal start of type” and “variable declaration not allowed here” errors in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CellFormatter.java`, indicating a malformed insertion of new code.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A libFuzzer run timed out after ~[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m s.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The full thread dump shows the main thread continuously in a native callback [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`traceConstCmpInt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, invoked from `CellFormatter.format`.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The hotspot is the nested loops in `CellFormatter.format` that search [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustively through all numerator/denominator pairs up to [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength – leading[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto very expensive computation when `denomLength` is large.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Observations from the Thread Dump  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The main thread’s CPU time is ~[0m[1;36m26[0m[39m s of a [0m[1;36m29.8[0m[39m s run, suggesting the format [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic never returns quickly.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no evidence of deadlocks or JVM GC stalls – the issue is pure [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCPU-bound work in the fraction formatting.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduced `MAX_DENOMINATOR_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m` to cap the search space.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Added a private static method `[0m[1;35mapproximateFraction[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble value, int [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxDenominator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` implementing a continued-fraction approach.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `[0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, replaced the nested loops with a call to [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mapproximateFraction[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecPart, maxDenominator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, unpacking its results into [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`currNum`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`currDenom`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All new code was inserted around lines [0m[1;36m35[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m70[0m[39m of `CellFormatter.java`.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Result and Compilation Errors  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The build logs report dozens of syntax errors such as “illegal start of type,”[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“variable declaration not allowed here,” and missing semicolons.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These errors span the region where the new constants, method, and modified [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`format` body were added.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The errors indicate that the patch’s added lines are not properly nested [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the class or method bodies [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., misplaced braces or annotations, incorrect[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindentation causing the compiler to parse method code at class scope[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Recommended Investigation Areas  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **CellFormatter.java Structure**: Verify class-level vs. method-level brace [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malignment. Ensure the new `approximateFraction` method and `MAX_DENOMINATOR_LENGTH`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstant are declared within the class but outside any other method.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Imports and Pattern Grouping**: Confirm necessary imports [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`java.util.regex.Matcher`, `java.util.regex.Pattern`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are in place and that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe inserted code does not disrupt existing imports or package declarations.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Method Body Boundaries**: Check that the original `[0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mopening and closing braces properly encompass the modified code, and that the new [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode does not break the method’s signature or return path.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Build and Style Conventions**: Review project code style [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline separators, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindentation, use of line continuations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure the patch follows expected [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatterns and that no stray markers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., line numbers like “40a:”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo root-cause speculation or corrective solutions are provided here; this report [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Understand the root cause  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The original fuzzer timeout stems from the brute-force nested loops in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCellFormatter.format, which search all numerator/denominator combinations up to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The last patch correctly switched to a continued-fraction approach [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mapproximateFraction[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but introduced dozens of syntax errors because the inserted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode included stray line-number prefixes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., “40a:”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and was malformed with [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrespect to Java’s class/method brace structure.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Reapply the performance patch cleanly  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. At the class level [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimmediately after the existing field declarations, i.e. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter line [0m[1;36m39[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Insert a new constant to cap denominator length:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         private static final int MAX_DENOMINATOR_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Insert the continued-fraction algorithm as a private static method:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         private static int[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m [0m[1;35mapproximateFraction[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble value, int maxDenominator[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             int sign = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             value = [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mDouble.isNaN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mDouble.isInfinite[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 return new int[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             int num0 = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, num1 = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, den0 = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, den1 = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             double x = value;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 int a = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mMath.floor[0m[1;39m([0m[39mx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 int den2 = a * den1 + den0;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mden2 > maxDenominator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                     break;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 int num2 = a * num1 + num0;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 num0 = num1; num1 = num2;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 den0 = den1; den1 = den2;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 double fracPart = x - a;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfracPart == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                     break;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 x = [0m[1;36m1.0[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[39m fracPart;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m choose the closer of the last two convergents[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             double err1 = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mden1 != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m num1 [0m[35m/[0m[39m den1 - value[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m : [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDouble.MAX_VALUE;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             double err0 = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mden0 != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;35mMath.abs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m num0 [0m[35m/[0m[39m den0 - value[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m : [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDouble.MAX_VALUE;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             int finalNum = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mden1 != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && err1 < err0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? num1 : num0;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             int finalDen = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mden1 != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && err1 < err0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? den1 : den0;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return new int[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m{[0m[39msign * finalNum, finalDen[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Within the [0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method, replace the brute-force section [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39moriginal lines [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m cap denominator length[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      denomLength = [0m[1;35mMath.min[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenomLength, MAX_DENOMINATOR_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m compute max denominator[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int maxDenominator = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m get best fraction via continued fractions[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      int[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m frac = [0m[1;35mapproximateFraction[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecPart, maxDenominator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      double currNum   = frac[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      double currDenom = frac[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Remove the declarations of minVal, the nested for-loops, and their associated [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdates to currNum/currDenom.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • Ensure currNum and currDenom are local to this block, matching the later [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatting logic.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The continued-fraction algorithm returns at most two convergents, matching the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprior exhaustive approach’s goal of choosing the closest approximation.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By capping denomLength with MAX_DENOMINATOR_LENGTH, we limit worst-case CPU [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musage.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing parsing, formatting, and fallback [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., returning the original [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcell on parse errors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain untouched.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Validate syntax and structure  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not include any “40a:”-style prefixes; these are patch metadata and must [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot be committed as code.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that both the new constant and the approximateFraction method are [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclared at class scope [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., between the existing field declarations and the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat method[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that braces match: one opening brace for approximateFraction is closed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore the format method’s signature.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that the format method’s opening brace precedes the trimmedCell logic,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand its closing brace is directly above the class’s final “[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m”.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Sanity checks  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compile CellFormatter.java after patch to ensure no “illegal start of type” or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“variable declaration not allowed here” errors.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing CSV parser unit tests to verify that standard formatting remains [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the fuzzer to confirm the timeout issue is resolved [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., format [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns quickly even for large denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side-effect mitigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new method uses only java.lang and java.util [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno new imports[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness or test code is modified; all API entry points remain the same.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If downstream code relies on the precise behavior of the exhaustive search [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39munlikely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the fraction returned by approximateFraction should be visually similar[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor typical denominator lengths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy cleanly reintroduces the performance-optimizing continued-fraction [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm without committing the malformed code that caused the compilation errors.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIt maintains all existing functionality, adheres to project style, and avoids [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtouching harness or test code.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
